\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Methods modeling the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_fauna_d_b}{Fauna\+DB}} query language. This class is intended to be statically imported into your code\+: 

{\ttfamily using static \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_fauna_d_b_1_1_query_1_1_language}{Fauna\+D\+B.\+Query.\+Language}};} 

Each of these methods constructs a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_fauna_d_b_1_1_query_1_1_expr}{Expr}}, which can then be composed with other methods to form complex expressions.
